计算机科学与技术（080901）
大连海事大学教务处
2024年9月
计算机科学与技术专业本科培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Computer Science and Technology Major
大连海事大学计算机大类专业包括计算机科学与技术、网络工程、软件工程、大数据科学与技术、人工智能技术五个专业。计算机类专业坚持“以成果为导向、学生为中心、持续改进”的办学理念，秉承“学汇百川，德济四海”校训，致力于国家与地方经济建设和行业发展需要，围绕厚基础、宽口径、高素质和强能力的人才培养目标，不断深化教育教学改革，培养具有家国情怀、国际视野、创新思维、自我学习和适应社会发展的复合型高素质专门人才。
计算机大类专业实施“1+3”通专结合的培养模式，学生入学后，进入前一年的不分专业的“大类培养”，修读通识教育课程与大类平台课程。后三年进入“专业培养”阶段，修读专业基础课程、专业核心课程，以及专业拓展课程，加强专业适应性。
The computer major at Dalian Maritime University includes five majors: computer science and technology, network engineering, software engineering, big data science and technology and artificial intelligence technology. Computer majors adhere to the educational philosophy of "results oriented, student-centered, and continuous improvement", adhere to the school motto of "learning from a hundred rivers, benefiting the four seas", and are committed to the needs of national and local economic construction and industry development. Focusing on the talent cultivation goals of thick foundation, wide caliber, high quality, and strong abilities, they continuously deepen education and teaching reform, cultivate patriotism, international perspective, and innovative thinking Compound high-quality specialized talents who learn and adapt to social development through self-learning.
The computer major implements a "1+3" training model that combines general education with specialized education. After enrollment, students enter the previous year's "general education" program regardless of their major, and take courses in general education and major platform courses. In the next three years, we will enter the stage of "professional training", taking basic courses, core courses, and expanded courses to strengthen our professional adaptability.
专业简介(Program Profile)
专业定位( Major Orientation)
计算机科学与技术专业有机结合学校的行业特色，立足服务国家信息产业布局和“一带一路”战略，课程设置和人才培养关注海上交通和智慧航运对信息技术人才的需求，培养具有良好职业道德、系统掌握计算机科学软硬件知识，具备解决复杂工程问题能力，拥有国际化视野和创新意识的高素质复合型人才，建设特色鲜明的国内一流专业。
The major of computer science and technology organically combines the industry characteristics of the school, based on serving the national information industry layout and the "the Belt and Road" strategy, curriculum and talent training pay attention to the needs of marine transportation and smart shipping for information technology talents, and cultivate good professional ethics, systematic grasp of computer science software and hardware knowledge, and the ability to solve complex engineering problems, High quality composite talents with an international perspective and innovative awareness, and building distinctive domestic first-class majors.
历史沿革( Major History )
计算机科学与技术专业成立于1977年，是我国1977年恢复高考后首批招生专业之一。1996年获得计算机应用技术硕士学位授予权，2002年获部、省共建计算机应用重点学科，2006年获批计算机应用技术博士点和计算机科学与技术一级硕士点，2018年获批省一流学科重点建设专业和计算机科学与技术一级博士点，2020获批省一流本科教育示范专业，2021年度通过国家工程教育专业认证，2022年度获批国家一流本科建设专业，2024年获批辽宁省基础学科拔尖学生培养计划2.0基地。
The Computer Science and Technology Major was established in 1977 and is one of the first majors to be enrolled in China after the resumption of the college entrance examination in 1977. In 1996, the Computer Science and Technology was granted the right to confer a master's degree in computer application technology. In 2002, it was jointly established as a key discipline in computer application by the Ministry and the Province. In 2006, it was approved as a doctoral program in computer application technology and a first-class master's program in computer science and technology. In 2018, it was approved as a first-class discipline key construction major and a first-class doctoral program in computer science and technology in the Province. In 2020, it was approved as a provincial first-class undergraduate education demonstration major. In 2021, it passed the national engineering education professional certification, and in 2022, it was approved as a national first-class undergraduate construction major.In 2024, it was approved as the 2.0 base of the Liaoning Province Basic Discipline Top Student Training Plan.
师资队伍(Teaching Staff )
本专业拥有专业和年龄结构合理，技术力量雄厚的稳定的师资队伍。现有全职教师35人，其中教授4人，副教授20人，讲师7人，实验师4人。其中有辽宁省教学名师1人，中科院百人1人。80%教师都有国内外知名高校博士学位，近50%教师有海外学习和工作经历。
This major has a stable teaching staff with a reasonable professional and age structure, strong technical strength. There are currently 35 full-time teachers, including 4 professors, 20 associate professors, 7 lecturers, and 4 experimenters. Among them, there is one renowned teaching teacher from Liaoning Province and one hundred students from the Chinese Academy of Sciences. 80% of teachers have doctoral degrees from well-known universities both domestically and internationally, and nearly 50% of teachers have overseas study and work experience.
专业特色(Professional characteristics )
本专业构建“夯实基础、强化能力、突出创新”的培养模式，大力开展课程改革与教学模式创新，强化培养学生的创新能力。学生在校期间可参加教师的科研项目，在教师指导下进行各种科技创新、科学研究和实验活动，并申请专利、发表科研论文。近三年，学生获得大量省级和国家级学科竞赛奖项。
专业落实“学生中心、成果导向、持续改进”教育理念，培养目标明确合理，毕业要求落实到位，课程体系合理，持续改进机制完善，学生培养质量符合工程教育认证的要求，得到了工程教育专业认证专家的肯定，用人单位对毕业生认可度高。
This major constructs a training model of "consolidating the foundation, strengthening abilities, and highlighting innovation", vigorously carries out curriculum reform and teaching mode innovation, and strengthens the cultivation of students' innovative ability. During their school years, students can participate in the teacher's research projects, conduct various technological innovation, scientific research, and experimental activities under the guidance of the teacher, and apply for patents and publish research papers. In the past three years, students have won a large number of provincial and national subject competition awards.
The major implements the educational concept of "student-centered, results-oriented, and continuous improvement", with clear and reasonable training objectives, effective graduation requirements, reasonable curriculum system, and perfect continuous improvement mechanism. The quality of student training meets the requirements of engineering education certification, and has been recognized by engineering education professional certification experts. Employers have high recognition of graduates.
招生规模(Enrollment Scale )
目前招生规模为三个自然班，约90余人。
At present, the enrollment scale is three natural classes with about 90 students.
通过本专业四年的学习，学生可以系统地掌握数学、自然科学知识、工程基础知识及计算机科学专业基础理论与技术知识，掌握基本科学方法，具有科学思维能力，能运用数学与自然科学基础知识解决实际问题。系统地掌握计算机硬件、软件及计算机应用的基本理论和应用技术，具备一定的项目实践能力和综合技术素质。具有口头和书面表达能力，并能在团队中发挥作用。具备通过继续教育或其它的终身学习途径拓展自己的能力，紧跟学科和专业发展。具有良好道德与修养，在科学研究、工程开发和应用实践中遵守法律法规，社会和环境意识强，可以进入IT行业从事软硬件系统应用开发方面的技术工作。
Through four years of study in this major, students can systematically master mathematics, natural science knowledge, basic engineering knowledge and basic theoretical knowledge of computer science, master basic scientific methods, have scientific thinking ability, and can use basic knowledge of mathematics and natural science to solve practical problems. Systematically master the basic theories and application technologies of computer hardware, software, and computer applications, and possess certain project practical abilities and comprehensive technical qualities. Have oral and written communication skills, and be able to play a role in the team. Possess the ability to expand oneself through continuing education or other lifelong learning pathways, closely following the development of disciplines and majors. Having good ethics and cultivation, complying with laws and regulations in scientific research, engineering development, and application implementation, with strong social and environmental awareness, can enter the IT industry to engage in technical work in software and hardware system application development.
二、培养目标(Program Objectives)
本专业认真贯彻党的教育方针，坚持立德树人，以培养德智体美劳全面发展的社会主义建设者和接班人为总目标，培养适应国家信息产业布局和“一带一路”战略，面向东北亚区域信息技术发展及智慧航运等相关行业发展需要，具有良好的学科素养和职业素养，能够胜任在物联网与嵌入式系统开发、大数据应用与云计算、人工智能等信息科学技术领域及交叉领域，进行计算机相关系统的分析与设计、建模与开发、管理与维护等工作，具有远大理想、家国情怀、创新精神和国际化视野的高素质创新型人才。
本专业培养学生具有职业素养能力、专业知识能力、项目协调与管理能力和职业提升能力等四个方面的计算机专业领域能力。
This major conscientiously implements the Party's education policy, adheres to building morality and cultivating talents, with the overall goal of cultivating socialist builders and successors with all-round development of morality, intelligence, physique, beauty and labor, and cultivates good disciplinary and professional qualities that adapt to the national information indeustry layout and the "the Belt and Road" strategy, and meet the needs of information technology development, smart shipping and other related industries in Northeast Asia, A high quality and innovative talents who are capable of analyzing and designing, modeling and developing, managing and maintaining computer related systems in the fields of information science and technology such as the Internet of Things and embedded system development, big data applications and cloud computing, artificial intelligence, and cross disciplinary fields, and possess lofty ideals, national sentiments, innovative spirit and international vision.
This major cultivates students' abilities in the field of computer science in four aspects: professional literacy, professional knowledge, project coordination and management, and career improvement.
具体指标如下：
培养目标1：具有良好的人文与社会科学素养、社会责任感和职业道德，身心健康，遵守法律法规、行业标准和规范，能够在相应技术工作中承担社会责任；
培养目标2：能够紧跟计算机相关技术发展，合理选取并熟练使用现代工具、主流软硬件平台，进行计算机复杂工程问题的需求分析、方案设计、模型建立、系统开发、管理和维护等相关工作，并考虑具体工程实践对环境和社会可持续发展的影响。
培养目标3：具有良好的团队合作精神和沟通组织能力，在团队中承担协调与管理工作，有能力领导一定规模的项目团队；
培养目标4：具有家国情怀，创新精神和国际视野，能不断学习更新知识并提高综合业务能力，适应社会发展和行业需求。
Specific indicators are as follows:
Training Objective 1: Have good humanistic and social scientific literacy, sense of social responsibility and professional ethics, be physically and mentally healthy, comply with laws and regulations, industry standards and norms, and be able to assume social responsibility in corresponding technical work;
Training objective 2: Be able to closely follow the development of computer related technology, reasonably select and proficiently use modern tools and mainstream software and hardware platforms, conduct requirement analysis, scheme design, model establishment, system development, management, and maintenance of complex engineering problems related to computers, and consider the impact of specific engineering practices on environmental and social sustainable development.
Training objective 3: Having a good team spirit and communication and organizational skills, responsible for coordination and management work within the team, capable of leading a project team of a certain scale;
Training objective 4: Having a sense of patriotism, innovative spirit, and international perspective, able to continuously learn and update knowledge, improve comprehensive business capabilities, and adapt to social development and industry needs.

计算机科学与技术专业(拔尖实验班)本科培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Computer Science and Technology (Top notch Experimental Class)
一、培养目标
I．Program Objectives
拔尖学生培养基地对标国内一流大学先进人才培养模式，着力培养立志于投身计算机基础科学研究的德智体美劳全面发展的创新型人才。该基地依托学校鲜明的航运特色和双一流建设交通运输工程学科，瞄准国家及辽宁重大战略需求、围绕海洋强国、交通强国建设需求，汇聚学校优势资源，着力培养具备设计开发复杂计算机软硬件系统和解决复杂工程实践问题的能力，具有良好人文素养、德才兼备、科学精神和创新能力的新时代经世致用领军人才。
The outstanding student cultivation base aims to benchmark against advanced talent cultivation models of first-class domestic universities, focusing on fostering innovative talents who are committed to scientific research field of computer science and are well-rounded in terms of morals, intelligence, physical, aesthetics, and labor education. Relying on the distinct characteristics in maritime and the “double world-class project” construction of transportation engineering discipline, the base targets the major strategic needs of the country and Liaoning province, and matches the requirements of building a powerful country in maritime and transportation. By gathering the advantageous resources of the university, the base strives to cultivate leading talents who are capable of designing and developing software and hardware of complex computer systems, solving complex engineering practical problems, possessing a good humanistic quality, moral and intellectual integrity, scientific spirit, and innovation ability.

后    记
培养计划是高等学校人才培养的纲领性文件，是教育思想和办学理念的集中体现，是实现人才培养目标的具体实施方案。根据学校质量体系文件《培养计划的制定与修订》（DMU-2-040）的要求，在多次校对、反复审核的过程当中，得到了各教学单位领导、教务、以及老师的大力支持和帮助。在此，对在培养计划修订过程中给予支持和帮助的各位，表示衷心的感谢。
培养计划的制定是一项繁琐的系统工作，难免会有疏漏，不足之处还望批评指正。培养计划的修订是以专业发展和知识更新为需求导向的，在执行过程中会进行细微调整。在此过程中，若产生分歧，应以教务系统为准。

本科专业培养计划
Undergraduate Program for
Marine Electrical and Electronic Engineering Major
[2024级适用]
软件工程（080902）
大连海事大学教务处
2024年9月
软件工程专业本科培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Software Engineering Major
一、专业简介
I．Program Profile
本专业创办于2005年，2021年建成辽宁省一流本科建设专业。依托软件工程学科和计算机科学与技术学科，师资力量雄厚，拥有软件工程基础实验室、软件工程综合实验室和软件测试实验室等多个专业实验室。通过项目驱动的教学与实践，培养学生的创新能力和实践能力。本专业培养学生熟练掌握从事软件需求分析、软件设计与实现、软件测试、软件维护和软件项目管理等工作所必需的基础知识、基本方法和基本技能。本专业毕业生既能在政府部门从事信息化建设和管理工作,也能在企事业单位从事软件项目开发和项目管理等工作,还能在计算机软件开发机构从事软件项目开发、软件测试、信息系统集成、软件产品销售和技术支持等工作。
This specialty was founded in 2005 and established as a first-class undergraduate construction major in Liaoning Province in 2021. Relying on the discipline of software engineering and that of computer science and technology, this specialty has featured strong faculty, professional laboratory of elementary software engineering, and comprehensive laboratory of software engineering and software testing laboratory, etc. Through project driven teaching and practice, students' innovation ability and practical ability are cultivated. This specialty trains students to master the basic knowledge, basic methods and basic skills for software requirement analysis, software design and implementation, software testing, software maintenance and software project management. The graduates can be engaged in the information construction and management work in government departments, can work at software development and project management in enterprises and institutions, and can work as software development, software testing, information system integration, software product sales and technical support in computer software development institutions.
二、培养目标
II．Program Objectives
本专业以立德树人为根本、服务国家战略和区域经济发展为目标，培养适应软件产业、交通信息服务业及相关行业领域发展需求，具有良好的科学素养和职业素养,具备设计开发复杂软件系统的能力、解决复杂软件工程问题的能力以及良好的沟通合作、组织管理能力，能够从事软件需求分析、软件设计与实现、软件测试、软件部署维护和软件项目管理等方面工作的工程技术人才，预期能够胜任软件工程教学科研、高级软件工程师、软件项目管理者和系统构架师等业务岗位工作。
本专业培养学生具有职业素养能力、专业知识能力、项目协调与管理能力和职业提升能力等四个方面的软件工程专业领域能力。毕业五年能达到：
培养目标1：具备良好的人文社会科学素养、社会责任感与职业道德，身心健康，诚实守信，遵守法律法规、行业标准和规范；
培养目标2：能够综合运用工程知识解决软件需求获取与描述、软件架构设计/软件结构优化、软件测试、软件维护过程和软件项目管理等复杂软件工程问题，达到具有国际水准的软件工程师或软件项目管理者的能力，并在设计开发和运维管理中考虑环境与社会影响；
培养目标3：能有效沟通和交流，在团队中发挥有效作用。能够在多学科背景下承担个体、团队成员和负责人的角色，体现出良好的团队合作精神及组织、协调、管理能力；
培养目标4：具有创新精神和国际视野，不断学习提升自己以适应社会发展。
This specialty takes cultivating virtue and nurturing talents as its fundamental goal, serving national strategies and regional economic development. In order to meet the development needs of software industry, traffic information service industry and related industries, this program cultivates good scientific literacy and professional quality, Engineering and technical personnel with the ability to design and develop complex software systems, solve complex software engineering problems, good communication and cooperation, organization and management capabilities, and be able to engage in software requirements analysis, software design and implementation, software testing, software deployment and maintenance, and software project management, etc., are expected to be competent for teaching and research of software engineering, Senior Software Engineer, software project manager and system architect .
This specialty cultivates students' abilities in the field of software engineering in four aspects: professional literacy, professional knowledge, project coordination and management, and career improvement. Five years after graduation, graduates should achieve the following abilities:
Training Objective 1: With good humanities and social science literacy, social responsibility and professional ethics, physical and mental health, honesty and trustworthiness, abide by laws and regulations, industry standards and norms;
Training Objective 2: Utilize engineering knowledge to solve complex software engineering problems such as software requirements acquisition and description, software architecture design / software structure optimization, software testing, software maintenance process and software project management, and achieve the ability of software engineers or software project managers with international standards, and consider environmental and social impacts in design, development and operation and maintenance management;
Training Objective 3: Communicate effectively and play an effective role in the team. Take on the role of individual, team member and leader under the background of multi-disciplinary, and show good team spirit and ability of organization, coordination and management;
Training Objective 4: Have the spirit of innovation and international vision, constantly learn and improve themselves to adapt to social development.
三、毕业要求
III．Program Requirements
本专业学生毕业时应掌握和具备以下几方面的知识与能力：
Our Graduate Attribute Profile has 12 elements, supported by a Knowledge Profile and a definition of the Level of Problem Solving, both given below:
1.工程知识：能够运用数学、自然科学、工程基础、专业基础和专业知识，解决复杂软件工程问题；
1.Engineering knowledge: Utilize the knowledge of mathematics, natural science, engineering foundation, professional basic and professional to solve complex software engineering problems;
2.问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学、工程科学和软件工程专业知识的基本原理，并通过文献研究，分析、识别软件工程领域的复杂工程问题，以获得有效结论；
2.Problem analysis: Apply the basic principles of mathematics, natural science, engineering science and software engineering professional knowledge, and through literature research, analyze and identify complex engineering problems in the field of software engineering, so as to obtain effective conclusions;
3.设计/开发解决方案：能够综合运用所掌握的专业知识、方法和技术，针对复杂工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的软件系统、模块或算法，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素；
3.Design/development of solutions: Comprehensively use the professional knowledge, methods and technology, design software systems, modules or algorithms to meet specific needs for solutions to complex engineering problems, and reflect the sense of innovation in the design process, taking into account factors such as society, health, safety, law, culture and environment;
4.研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对复杂软件工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验与实施实验、分析与解释数据，并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论；
4.Investigation: Based on the scientific principles and scientific methods, study the complex software engineering problems, including the design and implementation of experiments, analysis and interpretation of data and so on, and draw a reasonable and effective conclusion through information synthesis;
5.使用现代工具：能够针对复杂软件工程问题，开发或选用恰当的软件开发工具、建模工具、仿真工具和文献检索工具，完成复杂软件工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性；
5.Modern tool usage: Develop or select appropriate software development tools, modeling tools, simulation tools and literature retrieval tools for complex software engineering problems, complete the prediction and simulation of complex software engineering problems, and understand their limitations;
6.工程与社会：能够利用软件工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，客观地评价软件工程实践及复杂软件工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律和文化的影响，并理解其应承担的责任；
6.Engineering and society: Taking advantage of the relevant background knowledge in software engineering for reasonable analysis, objectively evaluate the impact of software engineering practice and complex software engineering problem solutions on society, health, safety, law and culture, and understand their responsibilities;
7.环境与可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对复杂软件工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响；
7.Environment and sustainability: Understand and evaluate the impact of engineering practice for complex software engineering problems on environmental and social sustainability;
8.职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养和社会责任感，能够在软件工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任；
8.Ethics: With humanities and social science literacy and sense of social responsibility, be able to understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in software engineering practice, and fulfill responsibilities;
9.个人和团队：能够适应多学科背景下的团队合作方式，并能在团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色；
9.Individual and teamwork: Adapt to the team cooperation mode under the multi-disciplinary background, and assume the role of individual, team member and person in charge in the team;
10.沟通：能够就复杂软件工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效的沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令，并具备一定的国际视野，能够进行跨文化背景的沟通与交流；
10.Communication: Communicate effectively with the industry peers and the public on the complex software engineering problems, including the writing of reports and the design of articles, statement, clear expression or response to an instruction. Have an international perspective and be able to communicate and communicate across cultures;
11.项目管理：理解并掌握软件工程项目管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中加以应用；
11.Project management and finance: Understand and master software engineering project management principles and economic decision-making methods, and apply these to multidisciplinary environment;
12.终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。
12.Life-long learning: Have the consciousness of independent learning and lifelong learning, and have the ability to constantly learn and adapt to development.
四、特色课程
IV．Feature Courses
面向对象分析与设计、软件设计与体系结构、人机交互导引、软件需求分析、软件质量保证与测试、.Net体系及编程、Java EE Web应用程序设计、Android平台应用开发技术、Oracle数据库应用技术、信息系统分析与设计、软件项目实践、移动应用开发课程实践和软件工程综合实训。

培养计划是高等学校人才培养的纲领性文件，是教育思想和办学理念的集中体现，是实现人才培养目标的具体实施方案。根据学校质量体系文件《培养计划的制定与修订》（DMU-2-040）的要求，培养计划原则上每4年修订一次，在特殊情况下可提前或推迟进行修订，我校培养计划上一次全面修订是于2021年进行，为满足教育教学改革的需要，我校今年组织对本科专业培养计划进行再次微调修订。
培养计划的制定是一项繁琐的系统工作，难免会有疏漏，不足之处还望批评指正。培养计划的修订是以专业发展和知识更新为需求导向的，在执行过程中会进行细微调整。在此过程中，若产生分歧，应以教务系统为准。

本科专业培养计划
Undergraduate Program for
Data Science and Big Data Technology Major
[2024级适用]
数据科学与大数据技术（080910T）
大连海事大学教务处
2024年9月
数据科学与大数据技术专业本科培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Data Science and Big Data Technology Major
一、专业简介
I．Program Profile
本专业依托计算机科学与技术学科，师资力量雄厚。通过项目驱动的教学与实践，培养学生的创新能力和实践能力。本专业培养学生熟练掌握面向大数据应用的数学、统计学、计算机科学的基础理论和方法， 熟练运用各种大数据分析技术和手段；系统学习数据分析、管理与应用、统计推断等方面的基本理论、方法和技能； 具备交通运输及其它领域大数据分析与应用开发的能力；具备良好工程素养、创新意识和团队精神。本专业毕业生可在交通运输领域及其它企事业单位，从事大数据分析、处理、开发和运维等方面的工作。
Data Science and Big Data major (DSBD) relys on the discipline of computer science and technology. This major has featured strong faculty and trains students to master the basic theories and methods of mathematics, statistics and computer science for large data applications, and skillfully use various large data analysis techniques and means. By systematically studying data analysis, management and application, statistical inference, and other aspects of the basic theory, methods and skills, students will own the ability of large data analysis and application development in transportation and other fields, and will possess good engineering quality, innovative consciousness and team spirit. In the field of transportation and other enterprises and institutions, the graduates can engage in large data analysis, processing, development and operation and maintenance, and so on.
二、培养目标
II．Program Objectives
本专业培养具有良好道德与修养，遵守法律法规，具有社会和环境意识，掌握数学与自然科学基础知识以及与计算系统相关的基本理论、基本知识、基本技能和基本方法，具有包括计算思维在内的科学思维能力和设计计算解决方案、实现基于计算原理的系统的能力，能清晰表达，在团队中有效发挥作用，综合素质良好，能通过继续教育或其他的终身学习途径拓展自己的能力，了解和紧跟学科专业发展，掌握数据科学与大数据技术专业的完整理论知识体系与应用分析技能。能够从事大数据有关教学、开发和应用的复合型技术人才。
The major aims to train high-quality specialized technical talents who have employment competitiveness in the research, development, deployment, and applications of computer systems and other related fields. Students are required to have good morals and cultivation, obey laws and regulations, have social and environmental consciousness, master the basic knowledge of mathematics and natural science and the basic theory, basic knowledge, basic skills and basic methods related to computing system. They are trained to obtain the ability of scientific thinking, including computational thinking, and the ability of designing calculation solutions and realizing the systems based on the principle of calculation. They are clutivated to be able to express clearly, play an effective role in the team, and have a good comprehensive quality. They are expected to expand their own ability through continuing education or other life-long learning ways, and understand and keep up with the development of the discipline. Students will master the complete theoretical knowledge system and application analysis skills of data science and big data technology major, and will be cultivated as the practical and complex technical talents who can engage in teaching, development and application of big data.
三、毕业要求
III. Graduation Requirement
数据科学与大数据技术专业学生毕业时应掌握和具备以下几方面的知识与能力：     Students graduated from the DSBD major should possess the following knowledge and abilities：
1. 工程知识： 能够运用数学、自然科学、工程基础知识和专业知识解决数据科学与大数据 技术领域复杂工程问题， 培育良好的科学、专业、人文素养和工程意识；
1. Engineering knowledge: Be able to apply mathematics, natural science, the basic knowledge of engineering, and professional knowledge to the solution of complex engineering problems in Data Science and Big Data Technology engineering field, and establish good scientific, professional, humanistic literacy and engineering awareness;
2.  问题分析： 能够应用数学、自然科学、工程基础和数据科学与大数据技术基本原理，通 过文献研究识别、表达和分析数据科学与大数据技术领域的复杂工程问题，获得有效结 论；
2. Problem analysis: Identify, express and analyze the complicated issues in the field of Data Science and Big Data Technology engineering by applying the basic principles of mathematics, natural science, engineering foundation, and intelligence science as well as by researching academic literature in order to obtain sound conclusions;
3. 设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对复杂数据科学与大数据技术工程问题的解决方案， 设计满足于特定需求的系统、程序或算法，并能够在设计环节中体现出创新意识， 考虑 社会、健康、安全、法律、文化、环境等问题；
3. Design/development of solutions: Design solutions for complicated Data Science and Big Data Technology engineering issues, including designing systems, programs, and algorithms that meet specific needs. Exhibit creativeness in the design process, taking society, health, security, law, culture, environment into considerations;
4. 研究：能够基于数据科学与大数据技术工程领域相关原理以及采用科学的方法通过设 计、实施实验方案， 分析、解释实验结果与数据对复杂的数据科学与大数据技术工程问 题进行研究，并通过综合各方面的信息得出合理有效的结论；
4. Investigation: Be able to study complex issues through designing, implementing experimental schemes, analyzing, interpreting experimental results and data, based on the related principles in the field of intelligence engineering and adopting scientific methods, and draw reasonable and effective conclusions by synthesizing all aspects of information;
5. 使用现代工具： 能够在解决数据科学与大数据技术工程领域复杂问题时，合理使用和开 发相关的技术、资源、程序、模拟软件、工程工具和信息技术工具等， 并理解其局限性;
5. Modern tool usage: Be able to solve complex engineering problems in the field of Data Science and Big Data Technology engineering, reasonably use and develop related technologies, resources, programs, simulation software, engineering tools and information technology tools, and understand their limitations;
6. 工程与社会：能够基于数据科学与大数据技术工程领域相关的工程背景知识进行合理分 析，评价数据科学与大数据技术工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、 法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任；
6. The engineering and society: Be able to conduct rational analysis based on relevant engineering background knowledge in the field of Data Science and Big Data Technology, evaluate the impact of Data Science and Big Data Technology engineering practices and complex engineering solutions on society, health, security, law and culture, and understand their responsibilities;
7. 环境与可持续发展： 能够理解和评价针对复杂数据科学与大数据技术工程问题的工程实 践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响；
7. Environment and sustainability: Understand and evaluate the sustainability and impact of engineering work in the solution of complex Data Science and Big Data Technology engineering problems in societal and environmental contexts;
8.  职业规范： 具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感， 能够在数据科学与大数据技术工程领 域的工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范， 履行责任；
8. Ethics: Have humanities and social science literacy, social responsibility, understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in the field of Data Science and Big Data Technology engineering, and fulfill their responsibilities;
9. 个人和团队： 具备良好的团队合作精神与责任意识，能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担 个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色；
9. Individual and teamwork: Have a good sense of teamwork and responsibility, and can play the role of individual, team member and leader in a multidisciplinary team;
10. 沟通： 能够就数据科学与大数据技术工程领域的复杂工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进 行有效沟通和交流， 具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流；
10. Communication: Be able to communicate effectively with their counterparts and the public on complex engineering issues in the field of Data Science and Big Data Technology engineering, have a certain international perspective, communicate with each other in a cross-cultural context;
11. 项目管理： 理解并掌握工程项目管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在解决数据科学与大数 据技术工程问题的多学科环境中应用；
11. Project management: Understand and master the principles of engineering project management and economic decision making, and apply them in the multidisciplinary environment to solve Data Science and Big Data Technology engineering problems;
12. 终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。
12. Life-long learning: Have the consciousness of independent learning and lifelong learning, and have the ability to study continuously and adapt to development.
四、特色课程
IV ．Feature Courses
Spark 大数据技术与应用、机器学习、商业智能与数据分析、分布式计算、人工智 能基础、智能信息检索、视觉信息理解与处理、应用统计学与 R 语言课程实践、大数据 平台与存储技术综合实践、大数据分析与可视化技术综合实训。
Spark Big Data Technology and Application，Machine Learning，Business Intelligence
and Data Analysis，Distributed  Computation，Artificial Intelligence Principle，Intelligent Information Retrieval，Visual information understanding and processing，Applied Statistics and R language Training, Integrated Practice of Large Data Platform and Storage Technology, Comprehensive Practical Training of Large Data Analysis and Visualization Technology.

本科专业培养计划
Undergraduate Program for
Network Engineering Major
[2024级适用]
网络工程（080903）
大连海事大学教务处
2024年9月
网络工程专业本科培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Network Engineering Major
一、专业简介
I．Program Profile
网络工程专业2006年成立并开始招生，隶属于大连海事大学计算机学科。该学科现有计算机科学与技术一级学科博士点、计算机科学与技术博士后流动工作站、计算机科学与技术一级学科硕士点。网络工程专业为2021年度省级一流本科建设专业(双万专业)，2023年软科全国排名15。该专业学生曾获得过2021年中国大学生年度人物入围奖（全国共101名），2021年中国大学生自强之星（全国共1842名），2021年辽宁省华育大学生年度人物（辽宁省共20名）等荣誉。网络工程专业的学科定位按照国外最新学科理论，根据中国计算机技术发展的规律和国情、民情，结合计算机技术市场对网络技术人员工作岗位的定位要求，将该专业定位在以计算机网络设计、维护与应用为根本，工程项目管理为拓展的专业门类。网络工程专业具备将计算机网与通信网（包括有线、无线网络）相结合的鲜明特色。突出网络工程专业的整体性；围绕网络安全与管理和网络编程两条主线培养学生的能力；课程设置覆盖了Windows、Linux、Unix三大操作系统平台。
Network Engineering major was established in 2006 and began to recruit students, which is affiliated to the computer discipline of Dalian Maritime University. The discipline has a doctoral program of first-level discipline of computer science and technology, a post-doctoral mobile workstation of computer science and Technology, and a master program of first-level discipline of computer science and Technology. The major of Network Engineering is the provincial first-class undergraduate construction major (double wan major) in 2021, and the soft major ranks 15th in 2021. Students of this major have won the 2021 Chinese College Student Person of the Year Award (101 nationwide), the Star of Chinese College Students in 2021 (1,842 nationwide), the 2021 Liaoning Huayu College Student Person of the Year (20 in Liaoning Province) and other honors. Network engineering major aims at computer network design, maintenance and application, it can be extended to professional major in engineering project management. This major will go with international latest scientific theory, based on the development of national computer technology and combined with the human resource requirement of network technique. The character of this major is the combination of computer network and communication network (include wired and wireless network) and show the integration of network engineering major. The ability of students will be trained with the knowledge of network security and management and network programming. The courses of this major are based on Windows, Linux and UNIX platform.
二、培养目标
II．Program Objectives
本专业培养具备网络工程基础理论、专业知识与应用能力，能从事计算机网络规划与设计、部署与实施、分析与测试、运行与管理以及应用开发等方面工作，并在工程实践中遵守职业道德和规范，富有创新、法律与环境意识，具有团队精神、持续学习能力与国际视野，能够成为德智体美劳全面发展的高素质创新型人才，成为社会主义事业优秀建设者和接班人。
上述培养目标可具体表述为以下四个子项：
培养目标 1：能够熟练运用数学与自然科学、工程基础知识，以及电子、计算机、网络等专业知识；能够从事计算机网络规划与设计、部署与实施、分析与测试、运行与管理以及应用开发等方面工作；
培养目标 2：具备独立分析和解决复杂网络工程问题的能力，富有实践和创新能力，能够成为所在工作领域的高素质创新型人才；
培养目标 3：具备高度的社会责任感和职业道德，德智体美劳全面发展，能在工程实践中考虑和评价社会、健康、安全、法律、环境及可持续发展等方面的问题，成为社会主义事业优秀的建设者和接班人；
培养目标 4：具有团队协作、组织协调和跨文化合作交流能力；具备自主和终身学习能力，不断提升自我，以适应社会经济发展的需要。
This major cultivates the students with the basic theory, professional knowledge and application ability of network engineering. And students can be engaged in computer network planning and design, deployment and implementation, analysis and testing, operation and management, and application development, and abide by professional ethics and norms in engineering practice, full of innovation, legal and environmental awareness, team spirit, continuous learning ability and international perspective, can become high-quality engineering and technical talents with all-round development of morality, intelligence, sports, beauty and labor, cultivate excellent builders and successors for the socialist cause.
The above program objectives can be specifically expressed as the following four sub-items:
Objectives 1: Students master and apply mathematics and natural science, the basic knowledge of engineering foundation, as well as electronics, computer, network and other professional knowledge, and engage in computer network planning and design, deployment and implementation, etc., analysis and testing, operation and management, and application development;
Objective 2: Students have the basic ability to analyze and solve complex network engineering problems independently, have the ability of practice and innovation, and be able to become a high-quality engineering and technical talent in the field of work;
Objective 3: Students have a high sense of social responsibility and professional ethics, develop morally, intellectually, physically, aesthetically and laboriously in an all-round way, and be able to consider and evaluate social, health, safety, legal, environmental and sustainable development problems in engineering practice, and become an excellent builder and successor of the socialist cause;
Objective 4: Students have the ability of team cooperation, organization coordination, and cross-cultural cooperation and communication, self-learning and lifelong learning to constantly improve themselves to meet the needs of social and economic development.

后    记
培养计划是高等学校人才培养的纲领性文件，是教育思想和办学理念的集中体现，是实现人才培养目标的具体实施方案。根据学校质量体系文件《培养计划的制定与修订》（DMU-2-040）的要求，本年度培养计划在2021年修订版基础上做了微调。在多次校对、反复审核的过程当中，得到了各教学单位领导、教务、以及老师的大力支持和帮助。在此，对在培养计划修订过程中给予支持和帮助的各位，表示衷心的感谢。
培养计划的制定是一项繁琐的系统工作，难免会有疏漏，不足之处还望批评指正。培养计划的修订是以专业发展和知识更新为需求导向的，在执行过程中会进行细微调整。在此过程中，若产生分歧，应以教务系统为准。

Intelligence Science and Technology Major

智能科学与技术（080907T）
大连海事大学教务处
2024年9月
智能科学与技术专业本科培养计划
Undergraduate Program for Intelligence Science and Technology Major
一、专业简介
I．Program Profile
大连海事大学智能科学与技术专业，2008年12月获教育部批准设立，2009年9月首次招生，是国内高校较早建立的智能科学与技术专业,隶属计算机学科与技术学科。2021年9月起，实施大类专业招生，招生规模约60人，2个班。截至2024年9月，有专任教师11名，实验教师2名，均有博士学位。其中博士研究生导师1人，硕士研究生导师8人。
专业以传授知识、培养能力、塑造价值、学生发展为目标，以计算机科学技术为基础，以智能科学理论、方法、技术为核心，注重培养学生良好的科学研究、技术应用、工程开发能力。专业特点为“以计算机为基础、侧重智能理论和方法、突出智能系统应用与开发，具有较高培养目标”，即以计算机科学与技术专业知识为基础；侧重传授设计开发智能软件、处理分析大规模、多模态数据的智能科学理论、方法知识；突出培养智能信息系统、智能机器人等智能系统的技术应用、工程开发能力；通过课程思政帮助学生塑造正确的世界观、人生观、价值观；结合学校交通和海事行业特色，培养服务于智能交通、智能航运、IT行业，能在智能类相关专业继续深造的高级复合型人才。
专业课程体系设置特点为“三层四递进”。“三层”指课程分“理工科公共基础课”、“计算机科学与技术专业基础课”、“智能科学与技术专业课”三个层次。“四递进”指“智能理论”、“智能方法和技术”、“智能系统”、“智能应用”四个递进层次。
专业拥有高水平实验室，如“脑与认知心理综合实验平台”、“小型足球机器人系统”、“机器感知综合实验平台”、“创新机器人综合实验平台”、“智能信息系统综合实验平台”、“数据仓库与数据挖掘实验平台”、“自然语言处理与信息检索综合实验平台”、“智能交通仿真系统平台”等。这些实验平台充分支撑新工科背景下的专业教学，并助力学生开展创新创业实践活动。
The Intelligence Science and Technology(IST) major of Dalian Maritime University, approved by Ministry of Education on December 2008, founded in 2009, and enrolled for the first time in September 2009. It is one of the earliest established IST major in domestic universities and is affiliated with the Computer Science and Technology discipline. Since 2021, it started to receive freshmen enrollment by large major, under the limit of 60 persons, 2 classes each year. As of September 2024, the IST has 10 faculty members, including 8 full-time teachers and 2 experimental teachers, all with doctorates. Among them, there are 1 supervisor for doctoral students and 8 supervisors for graduate students.
The major aims at imparting knowledge, cultivating abilities, shaping values, and student development. It is based on Computer Science and Technology discipline, with intelligent scientific theories, methods, and technologies as its core, and focuses on cultivating students' good scientific research, technology application, and engineering development capabilities. The major characteristics are "based on computers, focusing on intelligent theories and methods, highlighting intelligent systems and applications, and having high training goals." the specific meanings are as follows. (1) The IST is based on expertise of computer science and technology, and is focused on teaching the intelligent scientific theory and methods of the design and development of intelligent applications, processing and analysis of multi-modal big data. (2) It is focused on highlight the cultivation of technical application and engineering development capabilities of intelligent information systems, intelligent robots and other intelligent systems. (3) It is focused on helping students shape the correct views on the world, life and values through the curriculum ideology and politics. (4) Combined with the characteristics of the transportation and maritime, it is focused on cultivating senior comprehensive talents. The students with IST degrees are qualified for jobs in the intelligent transportation, the intelligent shipping industries, the IT industries, and for pursuit of the graduate degrees.
The characteristics of IST curriculum system are summarized as "three layers and four aspects". The so-called "three layers" means that all the courses are divided into "public basic courses"," computer science and technology specific courses" and "intelligence science and technology specific courses". The so-called "four aspects" refers to four levels including "intelligence theory, intelligent method and technology, intelligent system and intelligent applications ".
A high-level laboratory has been established in 2012. There are eight experiment platforms, including "brain and cognitive psychology comprehensive experiment platform", "small soccer robot system", "integrated machine perception experiment platform", "comprehensive innovative robot experiment platform", "integrated intelligent information system experiment platform"," data warehouse and data mining experiment platform", "natural language processing and information retrieval comprehensive experiment platform", and "intelligent transportation system simulation platform". IST students have many excellent experiment platforms to support their regular experiments and creative activities.
二、培养目标
II．Program Objectives
专业培养具有良好的科学素养和职业道德，扎实的数学、计算机和人工智能基础知识，系统地掌握智能科学与技术的基础理论与知识、技能与方法，具备智能信息处理、智能系统研究与开发能力，能在科研院所、企事业单位和政府机构从事智能科学与技术相关领域的研究、开发、应用和管理工作的高级复合型人才。
This major aim to educate advanced professionals with good integrative competence, professional morality, solid mathematics and professional knowledge of Computer Science & Technology and Artificial Intelligence. Students graduated from this specialty should master the principal theory and techniques about intelligence science & technology, have the essential researching and developing ability of intelligent information processing and intelligent systems, and suffice to serve academic，industrial or governmental departments.
三、毕业要求
III. Graduation Requirement
智能专业学生毕业时应掌握和具备以下知识与能力：
Students graduated from the IST major should possess the following knowledge and abilities：
1. 工程知识：能够运用数学、自然科学、工程基础知识和专业知识解决智能科学与技术领域复杂工程问题，培育良好的科学、专业、人文素养和工程意识。
1. Engineering knowledge: Be able to apply mathematics, natural science, the basic knowledge of engineering, and professional knowledge to the solution of complex engineering problems in intelligence science and technology engineering field, and establish good scientific, professional, humanistic literacy and engineering awareness.
2. 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学、工程基础和智能科学与技术基本原理，通过文献研究识别、表达和分析智能科学与技术领域的复杂工程问题，获得有效结论。
2. Problem analysis: Identify, express and analyze the complicated issues in the field of intelligence science and technology engineering by applying the basic principles of mathematics, natural science, engineering foundation, and intelligence science as well as by researching academic literature in order to obtain sound conclusions.
3. 设计/开发解决方案：对智能科学与技术复杂工程问题，能提出解决方案，能开发满足需求的软硬件系统，能在设计开发环节体现创新意识，并考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化、环境等因素。
3. Design/development of solutions: Design solutions for complicated intelligence science and technology engineering issues, including designing systems, programs, and algorithms that meet specific needs. In the meantime, exhibit creativeness in the design process, taking social, health, security, law, culture, environmental considerations into account.
4. 研究：能根据科学原理、运用科学方法，研究智能科学与技术领域复杂工程问题，包括设计实验、完成实验、分析数据、综合信息得到有效结论。
4. Investigation: Be able to study complex issues through designing, implementing experimental schemes, analyzing, interpreting experimental results and data, based on the related principles in the field of intelligence engineering and adopting scientific methods, and draw reasonable and effective conclusions by synthesizing all aspects of information.
5. 使用现代工具：能选用和开发现代工具，解决智能科学与技术领域复杂工程问题，并能理解工具的局限性。
5. Modern tool usage: Be able to solve complex engineering problems in the field of intelligence science and technology engineering, reasonably use and develop related technologies, resources, programs, simulation software, engineering tools and information technology tools, and understand their limitations.
6. 工程与社会：能运用智能科学与技术领域背景知识，分析评价工程实践和解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。
6. The engineering and society: Be able to conduct rational analysis based on relevant engineering background knowledge in the field of intelligence science and technology, evaluate the impact of intelligence science and technology engineering practices and complex engineering solutions on society, health, security, law and culture, and understand their responsibilities.
7. 环境与可持续发展：能理解和评价智能科学与技术工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。
7. Environment and sustainability: Understand and evaluate the sustainability and impact of engineering work in the solution of complex intelligence science and technology engineering problems in societal and environmental contexts.
8. 职业规范：有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能在智能科学与技术工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。
8. Ethics: Have humanities and social science literacy, social responsibility, understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in the field of intelligence science and technology engineering, and fulfill their responsibilities.
9.个人和团队：具备良好的团队合作精神与责任意识，能在多学科背景团队中承担个体、团队成员及负责人的角色。
9. Individual and teamwork: Have a good sense of teamwork and responsibility, and can play the role of individual, team member and leader in a multidisciplinary team.
10. 沟通：能与同行及公众有效沟通和交流，探讨智能科学与技术工程领域复杂工程问题，具备一定的国际视野，能在跨文化背景下沟通和交流。
10. Communication: Be able to communicate effectively with their counterparts  and the public on complex engineering issues in the field of intelligence science and technology engineering, have a certain international perspective, communicate with each other in a cross-cultural context.
11. 项目管理：理解并掌握工程项目管理原理与经济决策方法，能在多学科环境中运用。
11. Project management: Understand and master the principles of engineering project management and economic decision making, and apply them in the multidisciplinary environment to solve intelligence science and technology engineering problems.
12. 终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。
12. Life-long learning: Have the consciousness of independent learning and lifelong learning, and have the ability to study continuously and adapt to development.
四、特色课程
IV．Feature Courses
机器学习、人工神经网络及深度学习、模式识别、机器视觉、自然语言处理、智能信息处理、智能系统导论、数据仓库与数据挖掘、智能机器人、智能机器人实验、智能机器人操作系统、智能机器人程序设计、Android应用开发技术、移动应用开发课程实践、智能系统课程实践。
Machine Learning, Artificial Neural Networks and Deep Learning, Pattern Recognition, Computer Vision, Natural Language Processing, Intelligent Information Processing, Introduction to Intelligent Systems, Data Warehousing and Data Mining, Intelligent Robot, Intelligent Robot Experiments, Intelligent Robot Operating System, Intelligent Robot Programming, Android Application Development Technologies, Android Application Development, Intelligent System Implementation.

培养计划是高等学校人才培养的纲领性文件，是教育思想和办学理念的集中体现，是实现人才培养目标的具体实施方案。根据学校质量体系文件《培养计划的制定与修订》（DMU-2-040）的要求，培养计划原则上每4年修订一次，在特殊情况下可提前或推迟进行修订，我校培养计划上一次全面修订于2021年进行，为满足教育教学改革的需要，今年继续对本科专业培养计划进行微调。

[Table 2]
毕业要求1	工程知识：能够将数学、自然科学、工程基础知识、专业基础和专业知识用于解决复杂计算机工程问题。 Engineering knowledge: Be able to apply mathematics, natural sciences, engineering basic knowledge, professional foundation and professional knowledge to solve complex computer engineering problems.
毕业要求2	问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析复杂计算机工程问题，以获得有效结论。 Problem analysis: Be able to apply the basic principles of mathematics, natural science and engineering science to identify, express and analyze complex computer engineering problems through literature research, in order to obtain effective conclusions.
毕业要求3	设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对复杂计算机工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的系统、模块、算法或流程，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，综合考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化及环境等因素。 Design/Development Solutions: Be able to design solutions to complex computer engineering problems, design systems, modules, algorithms or processes that meet specific needs, and embody innovation awareness in the design process, taking into account social, health, safety, legal, cultural and environmental factors.
毕业要求4	研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对复杂计算机工程问题进行研究，包括设计实验、分析与解释数据，并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。 Research: Be able to study complex computer engineering problems based on scientific principles and scientific methods, including designing experiments, analyzing and interpreting data, and obtaining reasonable and effective conclusions through information synthesis.
毕业要求5	使用现代工具：能够针对复杂计算机工程问题，选择、使用与开发恰当的计算机技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂计算机工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。 Using modern tools: Be able to select, use and develop appropriate computer technology, resources, modern engineering tools and information technology tools for complex computer engineering problems, including prediction and Simulation of complex computer engineering problems, and to understand their limitations.
毕业要求6	工程与社会：能够基于计算机工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价专业工程实践和复杂计算机工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。 Engineering and Society: Be able to conduct rational analysis based on the background knowledge of computer engineering, evaluate the impact of professional engineering practices and complex computer engineering problem solutions on society, health, safety, law and culture, and understand the responsibilities to be undertaken.
毕业要求7	环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价复杂计算机工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。 Environment and Sustainable Development: Be able to understand and evaluate the impact of complex computer engineering practices on the sustainable development of the environment and society.
毕业要求8	职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养和社会责任感，能够在计算机工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。 Professional norms: Have humanities and Social Sciences literacy and social responsibility, can understand and abide by engineering professional ethics and norms in Computer Engineering practice, and fulfill their responsibilities.
毕业要求9	个人和团队：能够适应多学科背景下的团队合作方式，并能在团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。 Individuals and teams: Be able to adapt to the Multi-disciplinary Background of team cooperation, and can assume the role of individuals, team members and leaders in the team.
毕业要求10	沟通：能够就复杂计算机工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令，并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行交流。 Communication: Be able to communicate effectively with colleagues in the industry and the public on complex computer engineering issues, including writing reports and designing manuscripts, presenting statements, clearly expressing or responding to instructions, with a certain international perspective, and able to communicate in a cross-cultural context.
毕业要求11	项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。 Project management: Understand and master the principles of engineering management and economic decision-making methods, and can be applied in a multidisciplinary environment.
毕业要求12	终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。 Lifelong learning: Have the awareness of self-learning and lifelong learning, and the ability to constantly learn and adapt to development.

1.全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程 ，需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.  2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. [Table 5]
毕业要求1	具备数学、自然科学、计算机工程基础和专业知识，用于描述、分析和解决计算机系统、软硬件设计开发及计算机科学研究等相关复杂问题。 Possess knowledge of mathematics, natural sciences, computer engineering fundamentals, and specialized knowledge, which can be used to describe, analyze, and solve complex problems related to computer systems, software and hardware design and development, and scientific research computer science
毕业要求2	能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析计算机系统、软硬件设计开发以及计算机科学研究等复杂计算机工程问题，以获得有效结论。 Apply the basic principles of mathematics, natural sciences, and engineering to identify, express, and analyze complex computer engineering problems in computer systems, software and hardware design and development, and scientific research in computer science through literature study, and then aim to achieve effective conclusions.
毕业要求3	能够设计针对计算机系统、软硬件设计开发及计算机科学研究等相关复杂问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的计算机算法、模块、开发流程或软硬件系统，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识。 Provide solutions for complex problems related to computer systems, software and hardware design and development, and scientific research in computer science; design computer algorithms, modules, development processes, or software and hardware systems that meet specific requirements, and possess innovative thinking in the design process.
毕业要求4	能够基于计算机工程相关背景知识进行合理分析、评价计算机软硬件开发、系统设计等计算机工程实践过程和复杂计算机工程问题解决方案对法律、安全、健康、伦理和文化等影响，并理解应承担的责任。 Reasonably analyze and evaluate the impacts of computer hardware and software development, system design, and other computer engineering practice processes and complex computer engineering problem solutions on legal, safety, health, ethical, and cultural aspects, and understand the responsibilities that should be undertaken.
毕业要求5	能够适应多学科背景下的团队合作方式，并具备在团队中胜任需求分析、软硬件设计开发与测试等多种角色工作的能力。 Adapt to teamwork in a multidisciplinary context, and have the ability to perform various roles in a team, such as requirements analysis, software and hardware design and development, and testing.
毕业要求6	能够在复杂计算机工程问题与业界同行以及社会公众进行有效沟通，并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行交流。 Communicate effectively with peers in the industry and the public on complex computer engineering problems, possess international perspective, and be able to communicate in a cross-cultural context.
毕业要求7	具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，能够阅读理解、对比分析和综述计算机专业文献，能够发现实践中存在的问题，并具有不断学习新知识和适应计算机技术快速发展的能力。 Have a sense of autonomous learning and lifelong learning, be able to learn, compare, analyze, and summarize computer-related literature, identify problems in practice, and have the ability to continuously learn new knowledge and adapt to the rapid development of computer technology.
毕业要求8	具有人文社会科学素养、家国情怀和社会责任感，能够在计算机工程实践中遵守行业职业道德和规范，履行社会责任。 Possess humanistic and social science literacy, patriotism, and social responsibility, be able to adhere to industry professional ethics and norms in computer engineering practices, and fulfill social responsibility.

1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程 。其中，1）必修课不设“创新思维与创新方法”的专业需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成各专业规定的任选课学分。2）必修课设置“创新思维与创新方法”的专业需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成各专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, 1）The majors without "innovative thinking and innovative methods courses" in the training plan need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by each major.  2）The majors with "innovative thinking and innovative methods courses" in the training plan need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by each major. For specific courses, please refer to the list of elective courses in the course selection system of each year. 2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. For details, please refer to the regulations on student status management in the student handbook.	1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程 。其中，1）必修课不设“创新思维与创新方法”的专业需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成各专业规定的任选课学分。2）必修课设置“创新思维与创新方法”的专业需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成各专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, 1）The majors without "innovative thinking and innovative methods courses" in the training plan need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by each major.  2）The majors with "innovative thinking and innovative methods courses" in the training plan need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by each major. For specific courses, please refer to the list of elective courses in the course selection system of each year. 2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. 1.全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程 ，需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.   2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. 1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.    2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. For details, please refer to the regulations on student status management in the student handbook.	1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.    2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. 1. 工程知识: 具备用于解决复杂网络工程问题的数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识及其运用能力。	1-1、能够将数学和自然科学运用到复杂网络工程问题的恰当表述中。

1. 工程知识: 具备用于解决复杂网络工程问题的数学、自然科学、工程基础和专业知识及其运用能力。	1-4、能够将相关知识和数学模型方法用于专业工程问题解决方案的比较与综合。
2. 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析复杂网络工程问题，以获得有效结论。	2-1、问题识别：能够运用数学、自然科学和工程科学基本原理，对复杂网络工程问题进行识别，判断其关键环节
2. 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析复杂网络工程问题，以获得有效结论。	2-2、问题表达：能够基于相关科学原理和数学模型方法正确表达复杂网络工程问题
2. 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析复杂网络工程问题，以获得有效结论。	2-3、文献研究：能认识到解决问题有多种方案可选择，会通过文献研究来寻求可替代的解决方案
2. 问题分析：能够应用数学、自然科学和工程科学的基本原理，识别、表达、并通过文献研究分析复杂网络工程问题，以获得有效结论。	2-4、因素分析与方案分析：能运用自然科学、网络工程领域基本知识并借助文献研究，分析复杂网络工程问题的各种影响因素，获得有效结论。
3. 设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对复杂网络工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的网络应用系统或单元(模块)，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。	3-1、能够对复杂网络工程问题进行方案设计。
3. 设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对复杂网络工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的网络应用系统或单元(模块)，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。	3-2、能够对特定需求的网络应用系统或单元(模块)进行设计。

3. 设计/开发解决方案：能够设计针对复杂网络工程问题的解决方案，设计满足特定需求的网络应用系统或单元(模块)，并能够在设计环节中体现创新意识，考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。	3-4、在解决网络工程问题的设计环节中，能够考虑社会、健康、安全、法律、文化以及环境等因素。
4. 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对复杂网络工程问题进行研究，包括设计实施、测试、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。	4-1、调研能力：能够基于科学原理，通过文献研究或相关方法，调研和分析复杂网络工程问题的解决方案
4. 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对复杂网络工程问题进行研究，包括设计实施、测试、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。	4-2、实验设计：能够根据具体项目内容及对象特征，选择合适的研究路线，设计实验方案
4. 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对复杂网络工程问题进行研究，包括设计实施、测试、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。	4-3、实验实施：能够根据实验方案构建实验系统，安全地开展实验，正确地采集实验数据
4. 研究：能够基于科学原理并采用科学方法对复杂网络工程问题进行研究，包括设计实施、测试、分析与解释数据、并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论。	4-4、结果分析：能对实验结果进行分析和解释，并通过信息综合得到合理有效的结论
5. 使用现代工具：能够针对复杂网络工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂网络工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。	5-1、了解网络工程专业常用的现代仪器、信息技术工具、工程工具和模拟软件的使用原理和方法，并理解其局限性
5. 使用现代工具：能够针对复杂网络工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂网络工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。	5-2、能够选择和使用恰当的仪器、信息资源、工程工具和专业模拟软件，对复杂网络工程问题进行分析、计算与设计
5. 使用现代工具：能够针对复杂网络工程问题，开发、选择与使用恰当的技术、资源、现代工程工具和信息技术工具，包括对复杂网络工程问题的预测与模拟，并能够理解其局限性。	5-3、能够针对具体的对象，开发或选用满足特定需求的现代工具，模拟和预测专业问题，并能够分析其局限性
6. 工程与社会：能够基于网络工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。	6-1、工程背景知识：了解网络工程领域的技术标准体系、知识产权、产业政策和法律法规，理解不同社会文化对工程活动的影响。
6. 工程与社会：能够基于网络工程相关背景知识进行合理分析，评价工程实践和复杂工程问题解决方案对社会、健康、安全、法律以及文化的影响，并理解应承担的责任。	6-2、工程对社会的影响：能分析和评价网络工程实践活动对社会、健康、安全、法律和文化的影响，以及这些制约因素对项目实施的影响，并理解应承担的责任。
7. 环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对复杂网络工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。	7-1、理解理念：了解国家环境保护的法律法规，知晓和理解环境保护和可持续发展的理念和内涵。
7. 环境和可持续发展：能够理解和评价针对复杂网络工程问题的工程实践对环境、社会可持续发展的影响。	7-2 评价影响：能够站在环境保护和可持续发展的角度思考网络工程实践的可持续性，评价产品周期中可能对人类和环境造成的损害和隐患。
8. 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在网络工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。	8-1、人文社会科学素养：有正确价值观，理解个人与社会的关系，了解中国国情；
8. 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在网络工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。	8-2、职业道德和规范：理解诚实公正、诚信守则的工程职业道德和规范，并能在工程实践中自觉遵守。
8. 职业规范：具有人文社会科学素养、社会责任感，能够在网络工程实践中理解并遵守工程职业道德和规范，履行责任。	8-3、社会责任感：理解工程师对公众的安全、健康和福祉，以及环境保护的社会责任，能够在工程实践中自觉履行责任。
9. 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。	9-1、个体角色：能够在多学科背景下的团队中，基于自身专业特长，发挥个体优势，有独立开展工作的能力。
9. 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。	9-2、团队成员角色：能够在多学科背景下的团队中，与团队其他成员有效沟通，合作共事。
9. 个人和团队：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担个体、团队成员以及负责人的角色。	9-3 负责人角色：能够在多学科背景下的团队中承担负责人的角色，能够组织、协调和指挥团队开展工作。
10. 沟通：能够就复杂网络工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。	10-1、能就专业问题，以口头、文稿、图表等方式，准确表达自己的观点，回应质疑，理解与业界同行和社会公众交流的差异性。
10. 沟通：能够就复杂网络工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。	10-2、了解专业领域的国际发展趋势、研究热点，理解和尊重世界不同文化的差异性和多样性；
10. 沟通：能够就复杂网络工程问题与业界同行及社会公众进行有效沟通和交流，包括撰写报告和设计文稿、陈述发言、清晰表达或回应指令。并具备一定的国际视野，能够在跨文化背景下进行沟通和交流。	10-3、具备跨文化交流的语言和书面表达能力，能就专业问题，在跨文化背景下进行基本沟通和交流。
11. 项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。	11-1、掌握工程项目中涉及的管理与经济决策方法，了解工程及产品全周期、全流程的成本构成，理解其中涉及的工程管理与经济决策问题；
11. 项目管理：理解并掌握工程管理原理与经济决策方法，并能在多学科环境中应用。	11-2、能在多学科环境下(包括模拟环境)，在设计开发复杂网络工程问题解决方案过程中，运用工程管理与经济决策方法
12. 终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。	12-1、终身学习的意识：能在社会发展的大背景下，认识到自主和终身学习的必要性
12. 终身学习：具有自主学习和终身学习的意识，有不断学习和适应发展的能力。	12-2、终身学习的能力：具有自主学习的能力，包括对技术问题的理解能力，归纳总结的能力和提出问题的能力等，适应社会发展。

1.全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程 ，需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.  2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits. 1. 全校性选修课程分为人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程、创新与创业课程及其他课程。需要从人文与艺术课程、国家与社会课程、科学与技术课程分别选修至少2学分，同时需要完成专业规定的任选课学分。具体课程见每年度选课系统中的全校选修课程一览。 The elective courses are divided into “humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”, “science and technology courses”, “innovation and entrepreneurship courses ”and “other courses”.  Among them, need to take at least 2 credits from “Humanities and art courses”, “national and social courses”， “science and technology courses”， “innovation and entrepreneurship courses”, At the same time, it is necessary to complete the credits of elective courses specified by major.   2. 学生参加学校、院系组织的第二课堂活动，并符合学校有关学籍管理规定，可获得相应任选课学分，具体参考学生手册中的学籍管理规定部分。 If students participate in the second classroom activities organized by the school and departments, and meet the school's relevant regulations on student status management, they can obtain corresponding optional course credits.
